1 Overview
The TripXML Web Services are based on OTA specifications 2005A. Amadeus has made a few changes to the original OTA schemas to better fit its business needs. These changes are outlined in this document.
This document provides information on the following web services that are offered by TripXML:
o Travel build: creates a reservation in the provider system
o PNR cancel: cancels a reservation
o PNR read: retrieves a reservation
o Update: add, delete and modify elements in an existing reservation (PNR)
o Queue: provides queue management messages
o Queue read: retrieves a reservation from a specific queue
o Transfer Ownership: changes the ownership of a reservation
o Stored Fare build: create a stored fare record shell in a reservation
The document is based on the OTA messages user guide to help customers familiar with OTA specifications better understand the specific TripXML implementation.

All TripXML web services require the POS group of elements to be included in each request message, as defined below:
<POS>
<Source PseudoCityCode="YOUR PCC">
<RequestorID Type="21" ID="requestor"/>
</Source>
<TPA_Extensions>
<Provider>
<Name>GDS Name</Name>
<System>Target System</System>
<Userid>userid</Userid>
<Password>password</Password>
</Provider>
</TPA_Extensions>
</POS>

The POS data will be provided by the Amadeus support team.

2 Air suggested process flow



3 OTA_LowFarePlusRQ/RS
3.1 References
Web service URLs: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsLowFarePlus.asmx

WSDL: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsLowFarePlus.asmx?WSDL

3.2 Definition
The LowFarePlus method allows users to request fares and available flights based on an itinerary with departure and return dates. The response message returns available fares and flights that apply to those fares.

It is possible to narrow the search by providing optional search information:

o Preferred Vendor or Alliance code
o Preferred Cabin
o Time of departure with optional time window
o Direct, non-stop, number of connections
o Fare restrictions (advance purchase, min/max stay, penalty)
o Published, Private and negotiated fares
o Passenger types
The Low Fare Plus message returns up to 200 combinations of fare/flights.


3.3 Requesting different types of fares
It is possible with Low Fare Plus to request either Published or Private (negotiated) or Both (published and private) fares.
Example of Published fares for 2 passengers (1 adult and 1 child)

<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
</TravelerInfoSummary>

Example of Private fares for 2 passengers (1 adult and 1 child) on Amadeus

<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="JCB" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>

<PriceRequestInformation NegotiatedFaresOnly="true" PricingSource="Private"/>
</TravelerInfoSummary>

Example of Published and Private (Both) fares for 2 passengers (1 adult and 1 child)

<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="JCB" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
<PriceRequestInformation PricingSource="Both"/>
</TravelerInfoSummary>



3.4 Low Fare Plus Request message elements
TPA_Extensions specific to LowFarePlusRQ:
None Example 1:
MIA to NCE in economy cabin, restricted fares for 1 adult and 1 child.

<OTA_AirLowFareSearchPlusRQ>
<POS>
<Source PseudoCityCode="JNBZA2222">
<RequestorID Type="21" ID="requestor"/>
</Source>
<TPA_Extensions>
<Provider>
<Name>Amadeus</Name>
<System>Test</System>
<Userid>userid</Userid>
<Password>password</Password>
</Provider>
</TPA_Extensions>
</POS>
<OriginDestinationInformation>
<DepartureDateTime>2006-10-13T00:00:00</DepartureDateTime>
<OriginLocation LocationCode="MIA"/>
<DestinationLocation LocationCode="NCE"/>
</OriginDestinationInformation>
<OriginDestinationInformation>
<DepartureDateTime>2006-10-20T00:00:00</DepartureDateTime>
<OriginLocation LocationCode="NCE"/>
<DestinationLocation LocationCode="MIA"/>
</OriginDestinationInformation>
<TravelPreferences>
<FareRestrictPref>
<AdvResTicketing>
<AdvReservation/>
</AdvResTicketing>
<StayRestrictions>
<MinimumStay/>
<MaximumStay/>
</StayRestrictions>
<VoluntaryChanges>
<Penalty/>
</VoluntaryChanges>
</FareRestrictPref>

<CabinPref Cabin="Economy"/>
</TravelPreferences>
<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
</TravelerInfoSummary>
</OTA_AirLowFareSearchPlusRQ>


Example 2:
Low fare search for 2 adults on American Airlines from Miami to Honolulu. No fare restrictions.

<OTA_AirLowFareSearchPlusRQ>
<POS>
<Source PseudoCityCode="ABCD">
<RequestorID Type="21" ID="requestor" />
</Source>
<TPA_Extensions>
<Provider>
<Name>Amadeus</Name>
<System>Test</System>
<Userid>userid</Userid>
<Password>password</Password>
</Provider>
</TPA_Extensions>
</POS>
<OriginDestinationInformation>
<DepartureDateTime>2006-05-18T00:00:00</DepartureDateTime>
<OriginLocation LocationCode="MIA"/>
<DestinationLocation LocationCode="HNL"/>
</OriginDestinationInformation>
<OriginDestinationInformation>
<DepartureDateTime>2006-05-28T00:00:00</DepartureDateTime>
<OriginLocation LocationCode="HNL"/>
<DestinationLocation LocationCode="MIA"/>
</OriginDestinationInformation>
<TravelPreferences>
<VendorPref Code="AA"/>
<CabinPref Cabin="First"/>
</TravelPreferences>
<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="2"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
</TravelerInfoSummary>
</OTA_AirLowFareSearchPlusRQ>



3.5 Low Fare Plus Response message elements
TPA_Extensions specific to LowFarePlusRS:

o FlightDuration: provides flight segment duration.
o TotalJourneyDuration: provides the total journey duration for the flights.
o BookingClass: indicates the class of service to book for returned fare.

Example 1:

MIA to NCE in economy cabin, restricted fares for 1 adult and 1 child (limited display on 192 fares/flights returned).

<OTA_AirLowFareSearchPlusRS Version="1.001">

Example 2:
Low fare search for 2 adults on American Airlines from Miami to Honolulu. No fare restrictions.

The response is the same as the Low Fare example with the exception of the root element, called OTA_AirLowFareSearchPlusRS and up to 200 fares/flight returned instead of 9.

4 OTA_LowFareMatrixRQ/RS
4.1 References

Web service URL: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsLowFareMatrix.asmx

WSDL: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsLowFareMatrix.asmx?WSDL

4.2 Definition
The LowFareMatrix method allows users to request fares and available flights based on an itinerary with departure and return dates with a maximum of +3/-3 days range.
The response message returns a maximum of 49 available fares (and flights that search criteria).

Up to 49 fares are returned as it corresponds to 7 outbound days and 7 inbound days that are combined to provide the full response. If on some dates, there are no flights available then there will less than 49 fares returned.

Developers need to build a "matrix" type display correspondings to the fares returned. Here is an example of possible result display for a search


It is possible to narrow the search by providing optional search information:

o Preferred Vendor
o Preferred Cabin
o Time of departure with optional time window
o Direct, non-stop, number of connections
o Fare restrictions (advance purchase, min/max stay, penalty)
o Published, Private and negotiated fares
o Passenger types

Important note: once result matrix is displayed on a site and a user selects a "cell" that would correspond to specific outbound and inbound dates combination, it is advised to send another request, wsLowFarePlus, with those specific dates. That will allow customer to not only see the cheapest flight of the day, but as well to see other possible flight options for those specific dates.



4.3 Requesting different types of fares
It is possible with Low Fare Matrix to request either Published or Private (negotiated) or Both (published and private) fares.

Example of Published fares for 2 passengers (1 adult and 1 child)
<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
</TravelerInfoSummary>

Example of Private fares for 2 passengers (1 adult and 1 child) on Amadeus
<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
<PriceRequestInformation NegotiatedFaresOnly="true" PricingSource="Private"/>
</TravelerInfoSummary>

Example of Published and Private (Both) fares for 2 passengers (1 adult and 1 child)

<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
<PriceRequestInformation PricingSource="Both"/>
</TravelerInfoSummary>



4.4 Low Fare Matrix Request message elements
TPA_Extensions specific to LowFareMatrixRQ:
None Example 1:
JNB to CDG in economy cabin, restricted fares for 1 adult and 1 child.

<OTA_AirLowFareSearchMatrixRQ>
<POS>
<Source PseudoCityCode="OFFICEID">
<RequestorID Type="21" ID="requestor"/>
</Source>
<TPA_Extensions>
<Provider>
<Name>Amadeus</Name>
<System>Test</System>
<Userid>userid</Userid>
<Password>password</Password>
</Provider>

</TPA_Extensions>
</POS>
<OriginDestinationInformation>
<DepartureDateTime>2014-11-26T00:00:00</DepartureDateTime>
<OriginLocation LocationCode="JNB"/>
<DestinationLocation LocationCode="CDG"/>
</OriginDestinationInformation>
<OriginDestinationInformation>
<DepartureDateTime>2014-12-15T00:00:00</DepartureDateTime>
<OriginLocation LocationCode="CDG"/>
<DestinationLocation LocationCode="JNB"/>
</OriginDestinationInformation>
<TravelerInfoSummary>

</OTA_AirLowFareSearchMatrixRQ>




4.5 Low Fare Matrix Response message elements
TPA_Extensions specific to LowFareMatrixRS:

o FlightDuration: provides flight segment duration.
o TotalJourneyDuration: provides the total journey duration for the flights.
o BookingClass: indicates the class of service to book for returned fare.

5 OTA_LowFareScheduleRQ/RS
5.1 References
Web service URL: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsLowFareSchedule.asmx

WSDL: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsLowFareSchedule.asmx?WSDL


5.2 Definition
The LowFareSchedule method allows users to request fares and available flights based on an itinerary with departure and return dates.

The response message returns available fares and flights that apply to those fares sorted in ascending order of cheapest "from fare", applicable to each outbound flight.
Each outbound flight has a list of all applicable inbound flights with the exact fare when outbound and inbound flights are combined.

It is possible to narrow the search by providing optional search information:
o Preferred Vendor
o Preferred Cabin
o Time of departure with optional time window
o Direct, non-stop, number of connections
o Fare restrictions (advance purchase, min/max stay, penalty)
o Published, Private and negotiated fares
o Passenger types
The Low Fare Schedule message returns up to 200 combinations of fare/flights.


5.3 Requesting different types of fares
It is possible with Low Fare Schedule to request either Published or Private (negotiated) or Both (published and private) fares.
Example of Published fares for 2 passengers (1 adult and 1 child)

<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
</TravelerInfoSummary>

Example of Private fares for 2 passengers (1 adult and 1 child) on Amadeus

<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
<PriceRequestInformation NegotiatedFaresOnly="true" PricingSource="Private"/>
</TravelerInfoSummary>

Example of Published and Private (Both) fares for 2 passengers (1 adult and 1 child)

<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
<PriceRequestInformation PricingSource="Both"/>
</TravelerInfoSummary>



5.4 Low Fare Schedule Request message elements
TPA_Extensions specific to LowFareScheduleRQ:
None Example 1:
MIA to NCE in economy cabin, restricted fares for 1 adult and 1 child.

<OTA_AirLowFareSearchScheduleRQ>
<POS>
<Source PseudoCityCode="JNBZA2222">
<RequestorID Type="21" ID="requestor"/>
</Source>
<TPA_Extensions>
<Provider>
<Name>Amadeus</Name>
<System>Test</System>
<Userid>userid</Userid>
<Password>password</Password>
</Provider>
</TPA_Extensions>
</POS>
<OriginDestinationInformation>
<DepartureDateTime>2012-07-26T00:00:00</DepartureDateTime>
<OriginLocation LocationCode="MIA" />
<DestinationLocation LocationCode="NCE" />
</OriginDestinationInformation>
<OriginDestinationInformation>
<DepartureDateTime>2012-08-02T00:00:00</DepartureDateTime>
<OriginLocation LocationCode="NCE" />
<DestinationLocation LocationCode="MIA" />
</OriginDestinationInformation>
<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>1</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="1" />
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1" />

</AirTravelerAvail>
<PriceRequestInformation PricingSource="Both" />
</TravelerInfoSummary>
</OTA_AirLowFareSearchScheduleRQ>




5.5 Low Fare Schedule Response message elements
TPA_Extensions specific to LowFareScheduleRS:

o FlightDuration: provides flight segment duration.
o TotalJourneyDuration: provides the total journey duration for the flights.
o BookingClass: indicates the class of service to book for returned fare.

Example 1:
MIA to NCE in economy cabin, restricted fares for 1 adult and 1 child. (We have only displayed the first 6 outbound flights).

Notes:

- Each PricedItinerary element corresponds to one outbound flight (or outbound connecting flights).
- The first OriginDestinationOption includes:
o The outbound flight details.
o The cheapest "from" fare applicable to that outbound flight.
- The second OriginDestinationOption includes:
o The details of inbound flights that can be combined with previous outbound flight
o The exact total fare that applies to the combination of this inbound flight with the outbound flight
o The applicable classes of service to book for the outbound/inbound flights combination:
* FlightSegment/@ResBookDesigCode contains the inbound flight class of service
* OriginClass elements contain the class to book for the outbound flight (one OriginClass element per outbound connecting flight, the Index attribute indicating with outbound flight leg it applies to).
o The type of fare (Published or Private)
o The ValidatingCarrier information that needs to be carried on to the booking message



See response XML below:

6 OTA_AirFlifoRQ/RS

6.1 References
Web service URL: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsAirFlifo.asmx

WSDL: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsAirFlifo.asmx?WSDL

6.2 Definition
The AirFlifo method allows users to request flight information details based on a flight number. The response message returns real time operational data.


6.3 Air Flifo Request message elements
TPA_Extensions specific to AirFlifoRQ:
None Example 1:
Flifo request for flight AF 95.

<OTA_AirFlifoRQ Version="1.000">
<POS>
<Source PseudoCityCode="JNBZA2222">
<RequestorID Type="21" ID="requestor" />
</Source>
<TPA_Extensions>
<Provider>
<Name>Amadeus</Name>
<System>Test</System>
<Userid>userid</Userid>
<Password>password</Password>
</Provider>
</TPA_Extensions>
</POS>
<Airline Code="AF" />
<FlightNumber>95</FlightNumber>
<DepartureDate>2006-02-22</DepartureDate>
<DepartureAirport LocationCode="MIA" />
<ArrivalAirport LocationCode="CDG" />
</OTA_AirFlifoRQ>



Example 2:
Flifo request for flight JK 5129.
<OTA_AirFlifoRQ Version="1.000">
<POS>
<Source PseudoCityCode="JNBZA2222">
<RequestorID Type="21" ID="requestor" />
</Source>
<TPA_Extensions>

<Provider>
<Name>Amadeus</Name>
<System>Test</System>
<Userid>userid</Userid>
<Password>password</Password>
</Provider>
</TPA_Extensions>
</POS>
<Airline Code="JK"/>
<FlightNumber>5129</FlightNumber>
<DepartureDate>2006-02-22</DepartureDate>
<DepartureAirport LocationCode="FUE"/>
<ArrivalAirport LocationCode="MAD"/>
</OTA_AirFlifoRQ>


Example 3:
Flifo request for flight AC 918.
<OTA_AirFlifoRQ Version="1.000">
<POS>
<Source PseudoCityCode="ABCD">
<RequestorID Type="21" ID="requestor" />
</Source>
<TPA_Extensions>
<Provider>
<Name>Amadeus</Name>
<System>Test</System>
<Userid>userid</Userid>
<Password>password</Password>
</Provider>
</TPA_Extensions>
</POS>
<Airline Code="AC" />
<FlightNumber>918</FlightNumber>
<DepartureDate>2006-02-22</DepartureDate>
<DepartureAirport LocationCode="YYZ" />
<ArrivalAirport LocationCode="MIA" />
</OTA_AirFlifoRQ>



6.4 Air Flifo Response message elements
TPA_Extensions specific to AirFlifoRS:
None Example 1:
Flifo response for flight AF 95.

<OTA_AirFlifoRS Version="1.001">
<FlightInfoDetails TotalTripTime="0825">
<FlightLegInfo FlightNumber=" 95" JourneyDuration="08:25" FlightStatus="Arrived">

           <DepartureDateTime Scheduled="2006-02-22T17:40:00.0000000-05:00" Actual="2006-02- 22T17:38:00.0000000-05:00"/>
           <ArrivalDateTime Scheduled="2006-02-23T08:05:00.0000000-05:00" Estimated="2006-02- 23T08:00:00.0000000-05:00" Actual="2006-02-23T08:04:00.0000000-05:00"/>
<OperationTimes>
               <OperationTime Time="2006-02-22T17:38:00.0000000-05:00" OperationType="LEFT THE GATE" TimeType="Actual"/>

               <OperationTime Time="2006-02-22T17:52:00.0000000-05:00" OperationType="TOOK OFF" TimeType="Actual"/>
<OperationTime Time="2006-02-23T08:00:00.0000000-05:00" OperationType="ESTIMATED TIME OF
ARRIVAL" TimeType="Estimated"/>
<OperationTime Time="2006-02-23T07:52:00.0000000-05:00" OperationType="AIRCRAFT LANDED"
TimeType="Actual"/>
               <OperationTime Time="2006-02-23T08:04:00.0000000-05:00" OperationType="ARRIVED" TimeType="Actual"/>
</OperationTimes>
</FlightLegInfo>
<Comment>ENTIRE FLT- COCKPIT CREW AIR FRANCE</Comment>
<Comment>TO CDG  - ARRIVES TERMINAL 2C</Comment>
<Comment>MIA CDG - 9/ NON-SMOKING</Comment>
<Comment>MIA CDG - ET/ ELECTRONIC TKT CANDIDATE</Comment>
<Comment>MIA CDG - PERMANENT REQUEST / REQUEST ALL RESV G/U</Comment>
</FlightInfoDetails>
</OTA_AirFlifoRS>

               <OperationTime Time="2006-02-22T18:28:00.0000000-05:00" OperationType="Arrival" TimeType="Actual">

7 OTA_AirSeatMapRQ/RS

7.1 References
Web service URL: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsAirSeatMap.asmx

WSDL: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsAirSeatMap.asmx?WSDL


7.2 Definition
The AirSeatMap method allows users to request seat availability for a specific flight and specific cabin. The response message returns the seating layout of the plane with information for every seat.


7.3 Air Seat Map Request message elements
TPA_Extensions specific to AirSeatMapRQ:
None Example 1:
MIA to CDG with AF in economy cabin.

<OTA_AirSeatMapRQ>
<POS>
<Source PseudoCityCode="JNBZA2222">
<RequestorID Type="21" ID="requestor"/>
</Source>
<TPA_Extensions>
<Provider>
<Name>Amadeus</Name>
<System>Test</System>
<Userid>userid</Userid>
<Password>password</Password>
</Provider>
</TPA_Extensions>
</POS>
<SeatMapRequests>
<SeatMapRequest>
<FlightSegmentInfo DepartureDateTime="2006-10-11" FlightNumber="95">
<DepartureAirport LocationCode="MIA"/>
<ArrivalAirport LocationCode="CDG"/>
<MarketingAirline Code="AF"/>
</FlightSegmentInfo>
<SeatDetails>
<CabinClass CabinType="Economy"/>
<ResBookDesignations>
<ResBookDesignation ResBookDesigCode="Y"/>
</ResBookDesignations>
</SeatDetails>
</SeatMapRequest>
</SeatMapRequests>
</OTA_AirSeatMapRQ>

Example 2:

8 OTA_AirPriceRQ/RS
8.1 References
Web service URL: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsAirPrice.asmx

WSDL: http://amadeusws.tripxml.com/TripXML/wsAirPrice.asmx?WSDL

8.2 Definition
The wmAirPrice method allows users to request price information for specific flights and passenger types. The response message returns pricing information.

It is possible to specify optional supplemental information:

o Fare restrictions (advance purchase, min/max stay, penalty)
o Published, Private and negotiated fares
o Passenger types

8.3 Requesting different types of fares
It is possible with Air Price to request either Published or Private (negotiated) fares. Example of Published fares for 2 passengers (1 adult and 1 child)
<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
<PriceRequestInformation PricingSource="Published"/>
</TravelerInfoSummary>

Example of Private fares for 2 passengers (1 adult and 1 child) on Amadeus

<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="PFA" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
<PriceRequestInformation NegotiatedFaresOnly="true" PricingSource="Private"/>
</TravelerInfoSummary>

Example of "as booked" fares:
By defaulf the air price message returns the cheapest fare available for selected flights and it will return the classes of services that needs to be booked to get that fare. In that default mode, the classes returned can be different from classes requested.

It is possible to request the pricing "as is", meaning for the classes of service that are in the request. In that case the classes in the response will be the same as the classes in the request. To use the "as is" mode, request must contain the FareQualifier attribute with value "12" in it.
<TravelerInfoSummary>
<SeatsRequested>2</SeatsRequested>
<AirTravelerAvail>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="ADT" Quantity="1"/>
<PassengerTypeQuantity Code="CHD" Quantity="1"/>
</AirTravelerAvail>
<PriceRequestInformation FareQualifier="12" PricingSource="Published"/>
</TravelerInfoSummary>

9 OTA_AirRulesRQ/RS version 3

9.1 References
Web service URL: http://amadeusws.tipxml.com/TripXML/wsAirRules_v03.asmx

WSDL: http://amadeusws.tipxml.com/TripXML/wsAirRules_v03.asmx?WSDL


9.2 Definition
The wmAirRules method allows users to request fare rules text for specific flights itinerary. The response message returns fare rules information in text format.



9.3 Air Rules Request message elements
Example: fare rules for adult, child and infant


<OTA_AirRulesRQ>
<POS>
<Source PseudoCityCode="ATL1S2157">
<RequestorID Type="21" ID="Customer"/>
</Source>
<TPA_Extensions>

<System>Production</System>
<Userid>userid</Userid>
<Password>password</Password>
</Provider>
</TPA_Extensions>
</POS>
<AirItinerary>
<OriginDestinationOptions>

               <FlightSegment DepartureDateTime="2011-07-14T05:50:00" ArrivalDateTime="2011-07-14T06:55:00" FlightNumber="881" ResBookDesigCode="H">

<ArrivalAirport LocationCode="LHR"/>
<MarketingAirline Code="BA"/>
</FlightSegment>
               <FlightSegment DepartureDateTime="2011-07-14T13:35:00" ArrivalDateTime="2011-07-14T17:45:00" FlightNumber="209" ResBookDesigCode="H">

<MarketingAirline Code="BA"/>
</FlightSegment>
</OriginDestinationOption>

               <FlightSegment DepartureDateTime="2011-07-21T17:20:00" ArrivalDateTime="2011-07-22T06:40:00" FlightNumber="206" ResBookDesigCode="S">

<MarketingAirline Code="BA"/>

               <FlightSegment DepartureDateTime="2011-07-22T12:55:00" ArrivalDateTime="2011-07-22T19:55:00" FlightNumber="874" ResBookDesigCode="S">

<Paragraph>
<Text> CLASS OF SERVICE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THESE FARES APPLY FOR ECONOMY CLASS SERVICE.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> TYPES OF TRANSPORTATION</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	FARES GOVERNED BY THIS RULE CAN BE USED TO CREATE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	ROUND-TRIP/CIRCLE-TRIP/SINGLE OPEN-JAW/DOUBLE OPEN-JAW</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	JOURNEYS.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THESE FARES MAY NOT BE USED FOR INDIVIDUAL AND GROUP</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	INCLUSIVE TOURS.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARES ONLY APPLY IF PURCHASED BEFORE DEPARTURE.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> EXCEPTION-</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> MAY BE USED FOR EN-ROUTE UPGRADING FROM A LOWER</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARE PROVIDED ALL CONDITIONS OF THESE FARES ARE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> MET.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARES MAY NOT BE USED TO ESTABLISH A MTP</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FOR IT OR FLY-DRIVE PACKAGES.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> CAPACITY LIMITATIONS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> THE CARRIER SHALL LIMIT THE NUMBER OF PASSENGERS CARRIED</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> ON ANY ONE FLIGHT AT FARES GOVERNED BY THIS RULE AND SUCH</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARES WILL NOT NECESSARILY BE AVAILABLE ON ALL FLIGHTS.</Text>
</Paragraph>

<Paragraph>
<Text> THE NUMBER OF SEATS WHICH THE CARRIER SHALL MAKE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> AVAILABLE ON A GIVEN FLIGHT WILL BE DETERMINED BY THE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> CARRIERS BEST JUDGMENT</Text>
</Paragraph>
</SubSection>
<SubSection SubTitle="MIN STAY" SubCode="MN" SubSectionNumber="2">
<Paragraph>
<Text> TRAVEL FROM LAST INTERNATIONAL STOPOVER MUST COMMENCE NO</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> EARLIER THAN THE FIRST SUN AFTER DEPARTURE OF THE FIRST</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> INTERNATIONAL SECTOR.</Text>
</Paragraph>
</SubSection>
<SubSection SubTitle="MAX STAY" SubCode="MX" SubSectionNumber="3">
<Paragraph>
<Text> TRAVEL FROM LAST STOPOVER MUST COMMENCE NO LATER THAN 12</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> MONTHS AFTER DEPARTURE FROM FARE ORIGIN.</Text>
</Paragraph>
</SubSection>

<SubSection SubTitle="COMBINABILITY" SubCode="CO" SubSectionNumber="22">
<Paragraph>
<Text> ADD-ONS PERMITTED.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> END-ON-END</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  END-ON-END COMBINATIONS PERMITTED WITH DOMESTIC FARES.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  VALIDATE ALL FARE COMPONENTS. FARES MUST BE SHOWN</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  SEPARATELY ON THE TICKET. TRAVEL MUST NOT BE VIA THE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  POINT OF COMBINATION BETWEEN AREA 1 AND AREA 2.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  FARES. VALIDATE ALL FARE COMPONENTS. FARES MUST BE SHOWN</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  SEPARATELY ON THE TICKET. TRAVEL MUST BE VIA THE POINT</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  OF COMBINATION.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> OPEN JAWS/ROUND TRIPS/CIRCLE TRIPS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  FARES IN ANY RULE AND TARIFF.</Text>
</Paragraph>

<Paragraph>
<Text>  -TO FORM SINGLE OR DOUBLE OPEN JAWS.</Text>

<Paragraph>
<Text>	PERMITTED.</Text>

<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  -TO FORM ROUND TRIPS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  -TO FORM CIRCLE TRIPS</Text>

<Text>	PERMITTED.</Text>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  FARES MAY BE COMBINED ON A HALF ROUND TRIP BASIS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  -TO FORM SINGLE OR DOUBLE OPEN JAWS.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

<SubSection SubTitle="RULE APPLICATION" SubCode="RU" SubSectionNumber="1">
<Paragraph>
<Text>EUROPE TO AREA 1 SEMI-FLEX LEISURE ECONOMY FARES IN N/</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>S/V/L/M/K/H CLASS OR WORLD TRAVELLER PLUS FARES IN E CLASS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> APPLICATION</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> AREA</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THESE FARES APPLY</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	FROM AREA 2/AREA 3 TO THE UNITED STATES.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> CLASS OF SERVICE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THESE FARES APPLY FOR ECONOMY CLASS SERVICE.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> TYPES OF TRANSPORTATION</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	FARES GOVERNED BY THIS RULE CAN BE USED TO CREATE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	ROUND-TRIP/CIRCLE-TRIP/SINGLE OPEN-JAW/DOUBLE OPEN-JAW</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	JOURNEYS.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THESE FARES MAY NOT BE USED FOR INDIVIDUAL AND GROUP</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	INCLUSIVE TOURS.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARES ONLY APPLY IF PURCHASED BEFORE DEPARTURE.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> EXCEPTION-</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> MAY BE USED FOR EN-ROUTE UPGRADING FROM A LOWER</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARE PROVIDED ALL CONDITIONS OF THESE FARES ARE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> MET.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARES MAY NOT BE USED TO ESTABLISH A MTP</Text>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FOR IT OR FLY-DRIVE PACKAGES.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> CAPACITY LIMITATIONS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> THE CARRIER SHALL LIMIT THE NUMBER OF PASSENGERS CARRIED</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> ON ANY ONE FLIGHT AT FARES GOVERNED BY THIS RULE AND SUCH</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARES WILL NOT NECESSARILY BE AVAILABLE ON ALL FLIGHTS.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> THE NUMBER OF SEATS WHICH THE CARRIER SHALL MAKE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> AVAILABLE ON A GIVEN FLIGHT WILL BE DETERMINED BY THE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> CARRIERS BEST JUDGMENT</Text>
</Paragraph>

<SubSection SubTitle="RULE APPLICATION" SubCode="RU" SubSectionNumber="1">
<Paragraph>
<Text>EUROPE TO AREA 1 SEMI-FLEX LEISURE ECONOMY FARES IN N/</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>S/V/L/M/K/H CLASS OR WORLD TRAVELLER PLUS FARES IN E CLASS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> APPLICATION</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> AREA</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THESE FARES APPLY</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	FROM AREA 2/AREA 3 TO THE UNITED STATES.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> CLASS OF SERVICE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THESE FARES APPLY FOR ECONOMY CLASS SERVICE.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> TYPES OF TRANSPORTATION</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	FARES GOVERNED BY THIS RULE CAN BE USED TO CREATE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	ROUND-TRIP/CIRCLE-TRIP/SINGLE OPEN-JAW/DOUBLE OPEN-JAW</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	JOURNEYS.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THESE FARES MAY NOT BE USED FOR INDIVIDUAL AND GROUP</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	INCLUSIVE TOURS.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARES ONLY APPLY IF PURCHASED BEFORE DEPARTURE.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

<Text> EXCEPTION-</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> MAY BE USED FOR EN-ROUTE UPGRADING FROM A LOWER</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARE PROVIDED ALL CONDITIONS OF THESE FARES ARE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> MET.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARES MAY NOT BE USED TO ESTABLISH A MTP</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FOR IT OR FLY-DRIVE PACKAGES.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> CAPACITY LIMITATIONS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> THE CARRIER SHALL LIMIT THE NUMBER OF PASSENGERS CARRIED</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> ON ANY ONE FLIGHT AT FARES GOVERNED BY THIS RULE AND SUCH</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> FARES WILL NOT NECESSARILY BE AVAILABLE ON ALL FLIGHTS.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> THE NUMBER OF SEATS WHICH THE CARRIER SHALL MAKE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> AVAILABLE ON A GIVEN FLIGHT WILL BE DETERMINED BY THE</Text>
</Paragraph>

</Paragraph>

<Text>	</Text>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>

</Paragraph>

<Paragraph>

<Text>	OF THE NEWLY TICKETED FARE I.E. ADVANCE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	WHEN THERE ARE NO CHANGES TO THE FIRST FARE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	COMPONENT BUT OTHER FARE COMPONENTS ARE CHANGED.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THE ITINERARY MUST BE REPRICED USING FARES IN</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	EFFECT ON THE PREVIOUS TICKETING DATE -</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	OR - ON THE DAY OF REISSUE - WHICHEVER IS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	LOWEST.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THE NEW ITINERARY MUST MEET ALL THE RULE PROVISION</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	OF THE NEWLY TICKETED FARES SO THAT THE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	RECALCULATED FARE COULD HAVE BEEN USED FOR THE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	NEW ITINERARY IF THE PURCHASED ON THE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	ORIGINAL TICKET ISSUE DATE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	CHANGES AFTER DEPARTURE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THE ITINERARY MUST BE REPRICED USING FARES IN</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	EFFECT ON THE PREVIOUS TICKETING DATE. THE NEW</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	ITINERARY MUST MEET ALL THE RULE PROVISIONS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	OF THE NEWLY TICKETED FARES SO THAT THE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	RECALCULATED FARE COULD HAVE BEEN USED FOR THE NEW</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	ITINERARY IF PURCHASED ON THE ORIGINAL</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	TICKET ISSUE DATE</Text>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	UNLESS OTHERWISE SPECIFIED</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THE ORIGINAL CANCELLATION CHARGE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	WILL BE CARRIED FORWARD TO ANY REISSUED TICKET.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	WHEN THE ITINERARY RESULTS IN A HIGHER FARE THE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	DIFFERENCE WILL BE COLLECTED - AND- THE CHANGE FEE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	WILL BE APPLIED</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	WHEN THE NEW ITINERAY RESULTS IN A LOWER FARE THE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	CHANGE FEE WILL BE APPLIED - AND - NO REFUND</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	WILL BE MADE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	WHEN THIS FARE IS COMBINED WITH ANOTHER FARE THE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THE HIGHEST PENALTY OF ANY OF THE CHANGED FARE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	COMPONENTS WILL APPLY</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	FULL REFUND PERMITTED AT LEAST 24HRS BEFORE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	DEPARTURE IN CASE OF REJECTION OF VISA. EMBASSY</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	STATEMENT REQUIRED.</Text>

<Text>EUROPE TO AREA 1 SEMI-FLEX LEISURE ECONOMY FARES IN N/</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>S/V/L/M/K/H CLASS OR WORLD TRAVELLER PLUS FARES IN E CLASS</Text>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> CLASS OF SERVICE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	THESE FARES APPLY FOR ECONOMY CLASS SERVICE.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> TYPES OF TRANSPORTATION</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>

<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>

</Paragraph>

<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	EFFECT ON THE PREVIOUS TICKETING DATE -</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

</Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	EFFECT ON THE PREVIOUS TICKETING DATE. THE NEW</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>

<SubSection SubTitle="COMBINABILITY" SubCode="CO" SubSectionNumber="22">
<Paragraph>
<Text> ADD-ONS PERMITTED.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> END-ON-END</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  END-ON-END COMBINATIONS PERMITTED WITH DOMESTIC FARES.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  VALIDATE ALL FARE COMPONENTS. FARES MUST BE SHOWN</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  SEPARATELY ON THE TICKET. TRAVEL MUST NOT BE VIA THE</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  POINT OF COMBINATION BETWEEN AREA 1 AND AREA 2.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  END-ON-END COMBINATIONS PERMITTED WITH BA INTERNATIONAL</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  FARES. VALIDATE ALL FARE COMPONENTS. FARES MUST BE SHOWN</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  SEPARATELY ON THE TICKET. TRAVEL MUST BE VIA THE POINT</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  OF COMBINATION.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text> OPEN JAWS/ROUND TRIPS/CIRCLE TRIPS</Text>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  FARES IN ANY RULE AND TARIFF.</Text>

</Paragraph>

</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	MILEAGE OF THE LONGEST FLOWN FARE COMPONENT.</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  -TO FORM ROUND TRIPS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  -TO FORM CIRCLE TRIPS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	A MAXIMUM OF TWO INTERNATIONAL FARE COMPONENTS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>	PERMITTED.</Text>
</Paragraph>

<Text> OPEN JAWS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  FARES MAY BE COMBINED ON A HALF ROUND TRIP BASIS</Text>
</Paragraph>
<Paragraph>
<Text>  -TO FORM SINGLE OR DOUBLE OPEN JAWS.</Text>
</Paragraph>
